msg:Chengde is on a business trip, the first choice for a five-star hotel,
First, the price/performance ratio is too high.
The second is that it has just opened, the hardware is very new, and there is no smell like a new hotel, and the room has a fresh air system
Third, the sanitation is very clean, and my colleagues are a bit of a clean freak, but they are very satisfied
Fourth, because the surrounding area is close to the Wanda store, it is very convenient for eating and shopping.
Fifth, the supporting facilities are very good, there are many parking spaces, and the laundry and fitness are also good.
Sixth, the products produced by the restaurant are acceptable, both in taste and taste
The seventh is the front office manager and colleagues, who still have the demeanor of a star hotel, kind and professional. The restaurant team likes it, they have a sense of active service, because it is a banquet for friends, the meal arrangement is quite decent, and the price is not bad.
A satisfactory accommodation experience in Chengde

msg:I haven't been back to Chengde for a long time. I never thought that there are Wanda Plaza and Wanda Hotel in Chengde!
The hotel has just opened, and the lobby is full of luxury when you enter the lobby, and the service attitude of the front desk staff is very good. They helped us deliver three takeaways to the room haha, it's really troublesome for them.
We originally booked a deluxe twin room, but when we entered room 1813, we found that the air-conditioning system was broken, so we were upgraded to an executive twin room 2505. The room is much larger and it is on the other side of the square, which is quieter. comfortable~
The room is clean and hygienic, and the bedding is comfortable. I chose breakfast when I booked the room, and the breakfast variety is also very rich. My husband loves the lamb soup here. Overall, the experience of staying this time is very good, and I am very satisfied!
